FROM (
    SELECT [p].[Id], [p].[Author], [p].[CategoryId], [p].[ISBN], [p].[ImageUrl], [p].[ProductName], [p].[Publisher], [p].[StockAmount], [p].[UnitPrice]
    FROM [Products] AS [p]
    ORDER BY (SELECT 1)
    OFFSET @__p_0 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_1 ROWS ONLY
) AS [t]
INNER JOIN [Categories] AS [c] ON [t].[CategoryId] = [c].[Id]
